<item> <title>About http://enhanzphotography.com/about/ Sun, 15 Aug 2010 14:34:14 +0000 enhanzphotography http://enhanzphotography.wordpress.com/?page_id=2  
“The camera doesn’t make a bit of difference. All of them can record what you are seeing. But, you have to see.” -Ernst Haas

 

Enhanz Photography was established in 2010 by Hanz Lustre.

 

Offered Services:

Weddings
Debuts
Birthdays and Parties
Individual and Family Portraits (Studio or Outdoor)
Corporate Events
Product Shoots
Food Photography
Architectural/Structural Shoots
 
 
 

 
 
About Hanz:
At 15 years old, Hanz already took interest in photography. He joined basic and advanced photography classes back in 1996 and practiced it through his school publication. In 1999, he had the privilege to join a photojournalism and digital photography workshop with the Philippine Center for Photojournalism, instructed by well-respected photographers, Mel Cortez, Dennis Sabangan, Jimy Domingo, and Alex Baluyot. He was able to showcase this talent through the weekly newsmagazine, Pilosopong Tasyo. He was pre-occupied by his studies but he always had his passion for photography.
Hanz finished his Computer Science degree and worked in various professions. Despite the perks of the corporate world, he always had the yearning to practice photography. He was reunited with a former mentor,  to whom he served as an apprentice and soon enough, was shooting weddings at various locations.
He went through a more extensive and rigorous training under renowned (retired) wedding photographer, Lee Llamas. Fueled by his passion and love for his craft, he knows that he already has found what he wants to do in life.
